Happy Birthday Nimisha♥️

Tere is khaas din par, main tujhe dher saara pyaar bhejta hoon meri jaan Nimisha. Tu meri zindagi mein ek khaas jagah rakhthi hai, aur main hamesha tere saath hoon. Teri muskurahat meri duniya ko roshan karti hai.

Teri khushiyan meri khushiyan hain, aur main chahta hoon ki tu hamesha khush rahein. Jo bhi tu chahti hai, wahi meri dua hai ki tujhe mile.Aaj ke iss khaas din par, main aapko har khushi, har sapne ki poore aur har khushi ki dua karta hun. May your life be filled with endless love, laughter, and joy.

May this birthday be filled with laughter, joy, aur cherished memories jo hum hamesha yaad karenge. Main har ek moment ko cherish karta hun jo hum saath mein spend karte hain, aur main bekarari se intezaar kar raha hun un countless adventures ka jo aane wale saalon mein hamare intezaar kar rahe hain.
